RUS_SOV_establish_rk_UKR = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 202
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				UKR = { exists = yes }
			}
			UKR = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		202 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				202 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		UKR = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = UKR
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = UKR
				}
				remove_claim_by = UKR
			}
		}
		89 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		91 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		93 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		137 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		192 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		193 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		196 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		197 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		198 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		199 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		200 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		201 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		203 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		221 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		225 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		226 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		227 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		228 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		241 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		259 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		791 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		792 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		997 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1088 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1126 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1127 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1140 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1220 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1221 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1228 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1230 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1232 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1233 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1234 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1237 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1238 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1239 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1240 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1241 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1242 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1243 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1244 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1245 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1282 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1283 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1284 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1285 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		1286 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		202 = { add_core_of = UKR }
		release = UKR
		UKR = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = UKR
			}
		}
		UKR = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_SOV_UKR_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Workers Soviet"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Sovnarkom.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = red_junta_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = UKR
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 25
				totalist = 50
				radical_socialist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = "Workers Soviet"
				long_name = "Workers Soviet"
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		874 = { add_core_of = CHL }

						}

				}

			}

				long_name = "Workers Soviet"
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_SOV_establish_rk_RWA = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 869
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				RWA = { exists = yes }
			}
			RWA = { is_subject_of = RUS }
		}
		869 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } }
		OR = {
				869 = { NOT = { is_core_of = RUS } }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		RWA = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = RWA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = RWA
				}
				remove_claim_by = RWA
			}
		}
		869 = { add_core_of = RWA }
		release = RWA
		RWA = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = RUS
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = RUS} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = RWA
			}
		}
		RWA = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_SOV_RWA_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Workers Soviet"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Sovnarkom.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = red_junta_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = RWA
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}


			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 25
				totalist = 50
				radical_socialist = 25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = "Workers Soviet"
				long_name = "Workers Soviet"
			}
		}
	}
}
